## Summary

This PR implements Phase 1 of the Business Intelligence features for Discreet Courier SaaS platform. All features have been built, tested, and are ready for production deployment.

### Features Implemented

1. **Financial Dashboard** (`/admin/finances`)
   - Real-time revenue, expense, and profit tracking
   - Tax reserve calculator (25% automatic calculation)
   - Annual financial projections
   - Expense categorization and analysis
   - Monthly breakdown charts

2. **Client Preferences System** (`/admin/clients/[id]`)
   - Communication preferences (Email, Phone, SMS, WhatsApp)
   - Delivery instructions and special requirements
   - Important dates tracking (birthdays, anniversaries)
   - Relationship notes and history
   - Custom tag system for client categorization

3. **Dynamic Pricing Calculator** (Component)
   - Configurable pricing rules engine
   - Service tier multipliers (Standard, Express, VIP, White Glove)
   - Time-based premiums (business hours, after hours, overnight, holiday)
   - Urgency multipliers (1-3 hours, same day, next day, scheduled)
   - Real-time price calculation
   - Integrated into delivery creation flow

4. **CRM Lead Pipeline** (`/admin/leads`)
   - 6-column Kanban board (New, Contacted, Meeting Scheduled, Proposal Sent, Won, Lost)
   - Drag-and-drop lead management
   - Source tracking (Referral, Website, Social Media, Cold Outreach, Event, Other)
   - Follow-up date management
   - Lead value tracking
   - Notes and activity history

- **Framework**: Next.js 14.0.4 with App Router
- **UI Components**: shadcn/ui with Tailwind CSS
- **Icons**: Lucide React

## Summary

This PR implements Phase 1 of the Business Intelligence features for Discreet Courier SaaS platform. All features have been built, tested, and are ready for production deployment.

### Features Implemented

1. **Financial Dashboard** (`/admin/finances`)
   - Real-time revenue, expense, and profit tracking
   - Tax reserve calculator (25% automatic calculation)
   - Annual financial projections
   - Expense categorization and analysis
   - Monthly breakdown charts

2. **Client Preferences System** (`/admin/clients/[id]`)
   - Communication preferences (Email, Phone, SMS, WhatsApp)
   - Delivery instructions and special requirements
   - Important dates tracking (birthdays, anniversaries)
   - Relationship notes and history
   - Custom tag system for client categorization

3. **Dynamic Pricing Calculator** (Component)
   - Configurable pricing rules engine
   - Service tier multipliers (Standard, Express, VIP, White Glove)
   - Time-based premiums (business hours, after hours, overnight, holiday)
   - Urgency multipliers (1-3 hours, same day, next day, scheduled)
   - Real-time price calculation
   - Integrated into delivery creation flow

4. **CRM Lead Pipeline** (`/admin/leads`)
   - 6-column Kanban board (New, Contacted, Meeting Scheduled, Proposal Sent, Won, Lost)
   - Drag-and-drop lead management
   - Source tracking (Referral, Website, Social Media, Cold Outreach, Event, Other)
   - Follow-up date management
   - Lead value tracking
   - Notes and activity history

### Technical Details

- **Framework**: Next.js 14.0.4 with App Router
- **UI Components**: shadcn/ui with Tailwind CSS
- **Icons**: Lucide React
- **State Management**: React hooks
- **Build Status**: âœ… All 34 pages compiled successfully, 0 errors
- **Type Safety**: âœ… TypeScript strict mode passing

# Discreet Courier Columbus
 
**"One Driver. No Trace."**
 
Professional discrete courier and personal concierge service for Columbus, OH. From simple deliveries to VIP privacy-first services.
 
## ğŸŒŸ Features
 
### **4-Tier Service System**
 
1. **Standard Courier** ($35-50) - Document and package delivery
2. **Discreet Courier** ($50-75) - Confidential deliveries with privacy protection
3. **Personal Concierge** ($75-150/hr) - We buy, fetch, and handle tasks you cannot or prefer not to do
4. **The Fixer (VIP)** ($200-500/task) - Complex situations handled with absolute confidence and discretion
 
### ğŸ” **VIP Premium Features**
 
- **Cofre Humano (Human Vault)** - Secure storage of sensitive items, documents, and secrets

OK DE ENTRADA: LEIA TODO O HISTORICOS DO CH

OBSERVE QUE UMA CONVERSA GIGANTESCA PARA VOCE ANALIZAR, VAMOS FAZER O SEGUINTE, AGORA VOCE LE, ENTENDE E ORGANIZA COMO VAI IMPLEMENTAR, E DIGA SE ENTENDEU? DEPOIS DE VOCE DIZER QUE ENTENDEU DAREI UM "OK" PARA VOCE RELER E ANALIZR E VER SE PULOU, FALTOU, ESUQCEU, PASSOU RAPIDO DEMAIS, OU NÃƒO SE IMPORTOU DE ORGANIZAR, E ME DIR SE VOCE ACRESCENTOU ALGO? O PROXIMO "OK" VOCE FARA UMA AUTO-AUDITORIA, PARA TER 1000% DE CERTEZA QUE TUDO VAI VER IMPEMENTADO, O PROXIMO "OK" VOCE FARA O ROTEIRO, O PROXIMO "OK", VOCE FARA AS INFORMAÃ‡Ã•ES PARA O CASCADE/WINDSURF IMPLMENTAR, E DIRA PARA ELE FAZER TESTES, E CADA DESTE E IMPLEMETAÃ‡ÃƒO ELE VAI ANALIZAR, PARA O BUILDER NO VERSEL SEJA 100% APROVADO COM TODAS AS IMPLEMENTAÃ‡Ã•ES, FAÃ‡A GIT PARA GUARDAR AS INFORMAÃ‡Ã•ES DURANTE A IMPLEMENTAÃ‡ÃƒO E CASO DE ALGUM ERRO, SEJA MARCADO, PENSADO E CORRIGIDO SEMPRE.
IMPLEMETE TUDO, SEI QUE TEM MUITA COISA PARA ORGANIZAR PARA WINDSURF IMPLEMENTAR, NÃƒO QUERO RAPIDEZ, EU QUERO UM SAAS 1000% FUNCIONAL E QUE ESTEJA 1000% PRONTO PARA USO NO FINAL DA IMPLEMENTACÃƒO.
VOCE FARA A AULTIMA AUTO-AUTIDOTIA DELATHA E MINUCISA ANTES DE FINALER OS COMANDOS PARA O CASDADE/WINDSURF, SÃ“ DEPOIS DISSO, QUANDO VOCE ENTENDER QUE TUDO 100% ESTARA IMPLEMENTADO, VOCE ENTREGARA A MIM EDUARDO PARA EU COPIAR E COLAR NO WINDSURF.

# Discreet Courier Columbus
 
**"One Driver. No Trace."**
 
Professional discrete courier and personal concierge service for Columbus, OH. From simple deliveries to VIP privacy-first services.
 
## ğŸŒŸ Features
 
### **4-Tier Service System**
 
1. **Standard Courier** ($35-50) - Document and package delivery
2. **Discreet Courier** ($50-75) - Confidential deliveries with privacy protection
3. **Personal Concierge** ($75-150/hr) - We buy, fetch, and handle tasks you cannot or prefer not to do
4. **The Fixer (VIP)** ($200-500/task) - Complex situations handled with absolute confidence and discretion
 
### ğŸ” **VIP Premium Features**
 
- **Cofre Humano (Human Vault)** - Secure storage of sensitive items, documents, and secrets
- **Ãšltima Vontade (Last Will)** - Posthumous message/item delivery with configurable triggers
- **Guardian Mode 24/7** - Round-the-clock availability with direct line access

AIDA E PSCOLOGIA: 
The AIDA model (Attention, Interest, Desire, Action) is a cornerstone framework for structuring high-converting SaaS landing pages in 2025. It guides potential users from initial awareness to a final conversion point, such as a free trial or demo. 
1. Attention: The Hero Section
Capture focus within seconds to stop visitors from leaving. 
Catchy Headline: State your core value proposition clearlyâ€”what you do and who it's for.
Subheadline: Address a primary pain point or provide a specific, high-level benefit.
Visual Impact: Use professional product screenshots, short videos, or GIFs to show the software in action immediately. 
2. Interest: Features and Benefits
Maintain engagement by showing relevance to the user's specific problems. 
Benefit-Led Copy: Focus on how the software makes the user's life easier rather than just listing technical specs.
Quick Breakdown: Use bullet points or short sections to explain core features and unique selling points (USPs).
Educational Content: Incorporate a brief explanatory video or interactive element to demonstrate ease of use. 
3. Desire: Building Emotional Connection & Proof
Transition interest into a "need-to-have" feeling by establishing trust and value. 
Social Proof: Display customer logos ("As Seen On"), user counts, and specific testimonials to build credibility.
Case Studies: Link to or summarize data-driven success stories that highlight transformational results.
Value Reinforcement: Use a "we versus others" section to show clear differentiation from competitors. 
4. Action: The Conversion
Prompt the user to take a specific, frictionless next step. 
Clear CTAs: Use prominent, contrasting buttons with action-oriented text like "Start Your Free Trial" or "Book a Demo".
Strategic Placement: Repeat CTAs throughout the page so they are always accessible as the user scrolls.
Low Friction: Minimize form fields and clearly state if no credit card is required for a trial to reduce hesitation. 
SaaS-Specific Best Practices for 2025
Mobile Optimization: Ensure fast loading and "thumb-friendly" navigation, as mobile traffic continues to dominate.
Simplicity: Remove standard navigation bars on the landing page to keep the user focused solely on the conversion goal.
A/B Testing: Continuously test headlines, CTA colors, and copy using tools like Unbounce or Webflow to optimize the AIDA flow. 


SIGA: AlÃ©m da Psicologia das Cores e do Layout de Texto (Tipografia/GrÃ¡fica), sites, SASS e apps usam intensamente a Psicologia do UX/UI (ExperiÃªncia do UsuÃ¡rio/Interface), focando em usabilidade e design intuitivo, a Psicologia da PersuasÃ£o (HeurÃ­sticas) (gatilhos mentais), a Psicologia Cognitiva (como o cÃ©rebro processa informaÃ§Ã£o), e a Psicologia da Gestalt (percepÃ§Ã£o de padrÃµes), para criar interfaces que guiam, engajam e convertem, usando cores para emoÃ§Ã£o, layout para clareza e padrÃµes de design para facilitar a aÃ§Ã£o do usuÃ¡rio. 
Outras Psicologias Aplicadas em Digital:
Psicologia da Gestalt: Foca em como percebemos formas e padrÃµes. Essencial para agrupar elementos (proximidade, similaridade), criar hierarquia visual e guiar o olhar, usando espaÃ§os em branco (espaÃ§o negativo) para clareza.
Psicologia Cognitiva & Fitts' Law: Estuda como a mente processa. A Lei de Fitts, por exemplo, diz que o tempo para atingir um alvo depende da distÃ¢ncia e tamanho do alvo â€“ crucial para botÃµes e CTAs (Call-to-Actions).
Psicologia da PersuasÃ£o (Gatilhos Mentais): Usa princÃ­pios como escassez, urgÃªncia, prova social, autoridade para incentivar aÃ§Ãµes (compras, cadastros), muito comum em CTAs e landing pages.
Psicologia Comportamental (Behavioral Economics): Entende decisÃµes e vieses. Usa "nudges" (pequenos empurrÃµes) para guiar usuÃ¡rios, como a cor do botÃ£o de "Comprar" ou a sequÃªncia de um checkout.
Psicologia da AtenÃ§Ã£o: Como capturar e reter o foco. Design minimalista, contraste, e o uso de cores vibrantes em pontos especÃ­ficos (como um botÃ£o de "Cadastre-se") sÃ£o chaves aqui. 
Em Resumo para Sites/Apps/SaaS:
Cores: EmoÃ§Ã£o, identidade (Azul para confianÃ§a, Verde para crescimento).
Layout/Tipografia: Clareza, hierarquia (TÃ­tulos grandes, parÃ¡grafos curtos).
Gestalt: OrganizaÃ§Ã£o visual, agrupamento (elementos prÃ³ximos parecem relacionados).
AtenÃ§Ã£o/Cognitiva: Onde o olhar vai, quÃ£o fÃ¡cil Ã© usar (BotÃµes grandes e claros).
PersuasÃ£o: Incentivo Ã  aÃ§Ã£o (UrgÃªncia, benefÃ­cios claros). 
Todos esses elementos trabalham juntos para criar uma ExperiÃªncia de UsuÃ¡rio (UX) fluida e eficaz, transformando visitantes em usuÃ¡rios satisfeitos ou clientes.

```typescript
// BOOKING SYSTEM
interface BasicDelivery {
  pickupAddress: string;
  deliveryAddress: string;
  pickupTime: DateTime; // Scheduled ou ASAP
  packageDescription: string;
  contactPhone: string;
  contactEmail: string;
  specialInstructions?: string;
  price: number; // Auto-calculado baseado em distÃ¢ncia
}

// VALIDAÃ‡Ã•ES AUTOMÃTICAS
- MÃ¡ximo 6 deliveries por dia (hard limit)
- Booking mÃ­nimo 2h antecedÃªncia (ASAP = 2h)
- Raio mÃ¡ximo 25 milhas de Columbus centro
- Fora do raio: alerta automÃ¡tico + preÃ§o adicional
- Auto-reject se capacidade diÃ¡ria atingida
```

**SISTEMA DE COMUNICAÃ‡ÃƒO (Multi-canal):**

```typescript
// OPÃ‡ÃƒO 1: SMS (Americanos preferem)
Service: Twilio
- ConfirmaÃ§Ã£o de booking via SMS
- Updates de status via SMS
- "Picked up package - 10:35am"
- "On the way - 10:40am" 
- "Delivered - 11:05am"

// OPÃ‡ÃƒO 2: WhatsApp Business API
Service: Twilio WhatsApp / WhatsApp Business API
- Mesmas mensagens via WhatsApp
- Cliente escolhe canal preferido no booking

// OPÃ‡ÃƒO 3: Email
- ConfirmaÃ§Ã£o completa via email
- Updates cc'd via email
- Photo attachments

// OPÃ‡ÃƒO 4: In-App Notifications (se tiver app)
- Push notifications
- In-app messaging

// SISTEMA ESCOLHE AUTOMATICAMENTE:
if (customer.phone.startsWith('+1')) {
  primaryChannel = 'SMS';
  secondaryChannel = 'Email';
} else if (customer.phone.startsWith('+55')) {
  primaryChannel = 'WhatsApp';
  secondaryChannel = 'Email';
}
```

**PRICING AUTO-CALCULATOR:**

```typescript
function calculatePrice(pickup: Address, delivery: Address): number {
  const distance = getDistance(pickup, delivery);
  
  // Base price
  let price = 35;
  
  // Distance surcharge
  if (distance > 10) price += (distance - 10) * 2;
  
  // Outside coverage area
  if (distance > 25) price += 20; // Extra fee
  
  // Time-based surcharge
  const hour = new Date().getHours();
  if (hour > 18 || hour < 8) price *= 1.3; // After hours +30%
  
  // Weekend
  const day = new Date().getDay();
  if (day === 0 || day === 6) price *= 1.5; // Weekend +50%
  
  return Math.round(price);
}
```

**PHOTO PROOF OF DELIVERY:**

```typescript
// CUSTOMER PORTAL

- Email with photo attachment
- SMS with photo link
```

### **3. COMPRAS DISCRETAS ($75/hora)**

**Status:** 100% POSSÃVEL SOLO

**Sistema de Shopping Request:**

```typescript
interface ShoppingRequest {
  storeLocation: string;
  itemsList: string[]; // O que comprar
  budget: number;
  paymentMethod: 'reimbursement' | 'upfront'; // Cliente paga antes ou depois
  deliveryAddress: string;
  specialInstructions?: string;
  estimatedTime: number; // Auto-calculado
}

// AUTO-CALCULATION
function estimateShoppingTime(items: string[], store: string): number {
  const baseTime = 30; // 30min base
  const perItem = items.length * 5; // 5min por item
  const travelTime = getTravelTime(currentLocation, store) * 2; // Ida + volta
  
  return baseTime + perItem + travelTime;
}

// PRICING
const hourlyRate = 75;
const estimatedHours = estimateShoppingTime(...) / 60;
const price = Math.ceil(estimatedHours) * hourlyRate;
```

**PAYMENT HANDLING:**

```typescript
// OPÃ‡ÃƒO 1: Upfront
- Cliente paga orÃ§amento estimado via Stripe
- VocÃª usa pra comprar
- DiferenÃ§a Ã© reembolsada ou cobrada depois

// OPÃ‡ÃƒO 2: Reimbursement
- VocÃª usa seu cartÃ£o
- Cliente te reembolsa depois
```

```typescript
  // Auto-send notifications

  sendWhatsApp(customer.phone, getStatusMessage(status));
  sendEmail(customer.email, getStatusMessage(status));

  io.to(customer.id).emit('statusUpdate', {status, timestamp});
}
```

### **8. AGENDAMENTO / BOOKING SYSTEM**

**Status:** 100% POSSÃVEL (Totalmente AutomÃ¡tico)

**SISTEMA COMPLETO:**

```typescript
// CALENDAR INTEGRATION
Service: Google Calendar API

// Driver Calendar
- Synced com Google Calendar pessoal
- Blocos de tempo reservados automaticamente
- NÃ£o aceita booking se jÃ¡ ocupado

// Availability Check
function checkAvailability(requestedTime: DateTime): boolean {
  const deliveriesOnDay = getDeliveriesForDay(requestedTime);
  
  // Limite diÃ¡rio
  if (deliveriesOnDay.length >= 6) return false;
  
  // Conflito de horÃ¡rio
  const hasConflict = deliveriesOnDay.some(d => 
    isTimeConflict(d.pickupTime, requestedTime)
  );
  
  return !hasConflict;
}

// AUTO-ACCEPT / AUTO-REJECT
if (checkAvailability(booking.requestedTime)) {
  booking.status = 'accepted';
  addToCalendar(booking);
  sendConfirmation(customer);
} else {
  booking.status = 'pending';
  suggestAlternativeTimes(customer);
}
```

## ğŸ’° PRICING AUTOMÃTICO - LÃ“GICA COMPLETA

```typescript
function calculateDeliveryPrice(params: {
  type: 'basic' | 'confidential' | 'shopping',
  distance: number,
  datetime: DateTime,
  isRecurring: boolean
}): number {
  
  let basePrice = 0;
  
  // TYPE
  switch(params.type) {
    case 'basic': basePrice = 35; break;
    case 'confidential': basePrice = 55; break;
    case 'shopping': basePrice = 75; break; // Por hora
  }
  
  // DISTANCE
  if (params.distance > 10) {
    basePrice += (params.distance - 10) * 2; // $2 por milha extra
  }
  
  if (params.distance > 25) {
    basePrice += 25; // Fora da zona, surcharge adicional
  }
  
  // TIME
  const hour = params.datetime.hour;
  const day = params.datetime.day;
  
  // After hours (antes 9am ou depois 6pm)
  if (hour < 9 || hour >= 18) {
    basePrice *= 1.3; // +30%
  }
  
  // Weekend
  if (day === 0 || day === 6) {
    basePrice *= 1.5; // +50%
  }
  
  // RECURRING DISCOUNT
  if (params.isRecurring) {
    basePrice *= 0.9; // -10% discount
  }
  
  return Math.round(basePrice);
}
```

```typescript
interface BasicDelivery {
  pickupAddress: string;
  deliveryAddress: string;
  pickupTime: DateTime; // Scheduled ou ASAP
  packageDescription: string;
  contactPhone: string;
  contactEmail: string;
  specialInstructions?: string;

}

// VALIDAÃ‡Ã•ES AUTOMÃTICAS
- MÃ¡ximo 6 deliveries por dia (hard limit)
- Booking mÃ­nimo 2h antecedÃªncia (ASAP = 2h)
- Raio mÃ¡ximo 25 milhas de Columbus centro
- Fora do raio: alerta automÃ¡tico + preÃ§o adicional
- Auto-reject se capacidade diÃ¡ria atingida
```

```typescript
Service: Twilio

- "On the way - 10:40am" 
- "Delivered - 11:05am"

- Photo attachments

- In-app messaging

// SISTEMA ESCOLHE AUTOMATICAMENTE:

  primaryChannel = 'SMS';
```

**PRICING AUTO-CALCULATOR:**

```typescript
function calculatePrice(pickup: Address, delivery: Address): number {
  const distance = getDistance(pickup, delivery);
  
  // Base price
  let price = 35;
  
  // Distance surcharge
  if (distance > 10) price += (distance - 10) * 2;
  
  // Outside coverage area
  if (distance > 25) price += 20; // Extra fee
  
  // Time-based surcharge
  const hour = new Date().getHours();
  if (hour > 18 || hour < 8) price *= 1.3; // After hours +30%
  
  // Weekend
  const day = new Date().getDay();
  if (day === 0 || day === 6) price *= 1.5; // Weekend +50%
  
  return Math.round(price);
}
```

**PHOTO PROOF OF DELIVERY:**

```typescript
- Photo before pickup

- GPS coordinates embedded in photo metadata
- Timestamp embedded
- Auto-upload to cloud (S3/Cloudinary)

// CUSTOMER PORTAL
- Photos visible in customer dashboard
- Email with photo attachment
- SMS with photo link
```

### **3. COMPRAS DISCRETAS ($75/hora)**

**Status:** 100% POSSÃVEL SOLO

**Sistema de Shopping Request:**

```typescript
interface ShoppingRequest {
  storeLocation: string;
  itemsList: string[]; // O que comprar
  budget: number;
  paymentMethod: 'reimbursement' | 'upfront'; // Cliente paga antes ou depois
  deliveryAddress: string;
  specialInstructions?: string;
  estimatedTime: number; // Auto-calculado
}

// AUTO-CALCULATION
function estimateShoppingTime(items: string[], store: string): number {
  const baseTime = 30; // 30min base
  const perItem = items.length * 5; // 5min por item
  const travelTime = getTravelTime(currentLocation, store) * 2; // Ida + volta
  
  return baseTime + perItem + travelTime;
}

// PRICING
const hourlyRate = 75;
const estimatedHours = estimateShoppingTime(...) / 60;
const price = Math.ceil(estimatedHours) * hourlyRate;
```

```typescript
enum DeliveryStatus {
  PENDING = 'pending',
  ACCEPTED = 'accepted',
  EN_ROUTE_PICKUP = 'en_route_pickup',
  PICKED_UP = 'picked_up',
  EN_ROUTE_DELIVERY = 'en_route_delivery',
  DELIVERED = 'delivered',
  FAILED = 'failed'
}

// Driver atualiza status via mobile app (1 tap)
// Sistema auto-envia notificaÃ§Ã£o

function updateStatus(deliveryId: string, status: DeliveryStatus) {
  // Update database
  db.deliveries.update(deliveryId, {status, timestamp: now()});
  
  // Auto-send notifications
  sendSMS(customer.phone, getStatusMessage(status));
  sendWhatsApp(customer.phone, getStatusMessage(status));
  sendEmail(customer.email, getStatusMessage(status));
  
  // Update customer portal (real-time via WebSocket)
  io.to(customer.id).emit('statusUpdate', {status, timestamp});
}
```

### **8. AGENDAMENTO / BOOKING SYSTEM**

**Status:** 100% POSSÃVEL (Totalmente AutomÃ¡tico)

**SISTEMA COMPLETO:**

```typescript
// CALENDAR INTEGRATION
Service: Google Calendar API

// Driver Calendar
- Synced com Google Calendar pessoal
- Blocos de tempo reservados automaticamente
- NÃ£o aceita booking se jÃ¡ ocupado

// Availability Check
function checkAvailability(requestedTime: DateTime): boolean {
  const deliveriesOnDay = getDeliveriesForDay(requestedTime);
  
  // Limite diÃ¡rio
  if (deliveriesOnDay.length >= 6) return false;
  
  // Conflito de horÃ¡rio
  const hasConflict = deliveriesOnDay.some(d => 
    isTimeConflict(d.pickupTime, requestedTime)
  );
  
  return !hasConflict;
}

// AUTO-ACCEPT / AUTO-REJECT
if (checkAvailability(booking.requestedTime)) {
  booking.status = 'accepted';
  addToCalendar(booking);
  sendConfirmation(customer);
} else {
  booking.status = 'pending';
  suggestAlternativeTimes(customer);
}
```

**CUSTOMER BOOKING INTERFACE:**

```typescript
- Cliente escolhe
- ConfirmaÃ§Ã£o instantÃ¢nea

- NÃ£o pode escolher horÃ¡rio ocupado
```

## ğŸ’° PRICING AUTOMÃTICO - LÃ“GICA COMPLETA

```typescript
function calculateDeliveryPrice(params: {
  type: 'basic' | 'confidential' | 'shopping',
  distance: number,
  datetime: DateTime,
  isRecurring: boolean
}): number {
  
  let basePrice = 0;
  
  // TYPE
  switch(params.type) {
    case 'basic': basePrice = 35; break;
    case 'confidential': basePrice = 55; break;
    case 'shopping': basePrice = 75; break; // Por hora
  }
  
  // DISTANCE
  if (params.distance > 10) {
    basePrice += (params.distance - 10) * 2; // $2 por milha extra
  }
  
  if (params.distance > 25) {
    basePrice += 25; // Fora da zona, surcharge adicional
  }
  
  // TIME
  const hour = params.datetime.hour;
  const day = params.datetime.day;
  
  // After hours (antes 9am ou depois 6pm)
  if (hour < 9 || hour >= 18) {
    basePrice *= 1.3; // +30%
  }
  
  // Weekend
  if (day === 0 || day === 6) {
    basePrice *= 1.5; // +50%
  }
  
  // RECURRING DISCOUNT
  if (params.isRecurring) {
    basePrice *= 0.9; // -10% discount
  }
  
  return Math.round(basePrice);
}
```

### **2. ALTERNATIVAS AO WHATSAPP (Para Americanos)**

```typescript
// ============================================
// COMUNICAÃ‡ÃƒO: AMERICANOS vs LATINOS
// ============================================

/**
 * PROBLEMA: Americanos nÃ£o usam WhatsApp tanto quanto latinos
 * SOLUÃ‡ÃƒO: Priorizar SMS como primÃ¡rio, WhatsApp como secundÃ¡rio
 */

interface CustomerCommunicationPreference {
  primary: 'sms' | 'whatsapp' | 'email' | 'app';
  secondary?: 'sms' | 'whatsapp' | 'email';
  phoneNumber: string;
  email: string;
}

// AUTO-DETECT baseado em country code
function detectPreferredChannel(phone: string): 'sms' | 'whatsapp' {
  const countryCode = phone.substring(0, 3);
  
  if (countryCode === '+1') {
    // USA/Canada = SMS preferred
    return 'sms';
  } else if (['+55', '+52', '+54', '+51'].includes(countryCode)) {
    // Brasil, Mexico, Argentina, Peru = WhatsApp
    return 'whatsapp';
  }
  
  return 'sms'; // Default
}

// CANAIS DE COMUNICAÃ‡ÃƒO (Priority Order for Americans)

const COMMUNICATION_CHANNELS_US = {
  
  // 1. SMS (Twilio) - PRIMÃRIO para americanos
  sms: {
    service: 'Twilio',
    pros: [
      'Todo americano usa',
      'NÃ£o precisa de app adicional',
      'Delivery instantÃ¢neo',
      '98% open rate'
    ],
    cost: '$0.0079 per message',
    implementation: 'Twilio SDK'
  },
  
  // 2. Email - SECUNDÃRIO
  email: {
    service: 'SendGrid ou AWS SES',
    pros: [
      'GrÃ¡tis atÃ© 10k/mÃªs',
      'DocumentaÃ§Ã£o permanente',
      'Pode incluir attachments (receipts, photos)'
    ],
    cost: 'Free tier disponÃ­vel',
    implementation: 'SendGrid/SES API'
  },
  
  // 3. Push Notifications (Se tiver app)
  push: {
    service: 'Firebase Cloud Messaging (FCM)',
    pros: [
      'Instant',
      'Rich media',
      'Free'
    ],
    implementation: 'Firebase SDK',
    requires: 'Mobile app installed'
  },
  
  // 4. In-App Messaging
  inApp: {
    service: 'Stream Chat ou Sendbird',
    pros: [
      'Real-time',
      'Rich features',
      'Professional'
    ],
    cost: 'Free tier available',
    implementation: 'Stream SDK'
  },
  
  // 5. Voice Call (Automated)
  voice: {
    service: 'Twilio Voice',
    pros: [
      'Para updates crÃ­ticos',
      'Idosos preferem'
    ],
    cost: '$0.013/min',
    useCase: 'Emergency notifications only'
  }
};

// IMPLEMENTATION EXAMPLE

async function notifyCustomer(
  delivery: Delivery, 
  status: DeliveryStatus,
  customer: Customer
) {
  
  const message = getStatusMessage(status);
  
  // Multi-channel simultÃ¢neo
  await Promise.all([
    
    // SMS (PrimÃ¡rio para US)
    sendSMS({
      to: customer.phone,
      body: message,
      from: process.env.TWILIO_PHONE
    }),
    
    // Email (Backup)
    sendEmail({
      to: customer.email,
      subject: `Delivery Update: ${status}`,
      body: message,
      attachments: status === 'delivered' ? [proofOfDeliveryPDF] : []
    }),
    
    // Push (Se app instalado)
    customer.hasMobileApp && sendPush({
      userId: customer.id,
      title: 'Delivery Update',
      body: message,
      data: { deliveryId: delivery.id }
    }),
    
    // WhatsApp (Apenas se customer preferir)
    customer.prefersWhatsApp && sendWhatsApp({
      to: customer.phone,
      body: message
    })
  ]);
}
```

### **2. ALTERNATIVAS AO WHATSAPP (Para Americanos)**

```typescript
// ============================================
// COMUNICAÃ‡ÃƒO: AMERICANOS vs LATINOS
// ============================================

/**
 * PROBLEMA: Americanos nÃ£o usam WhatsApp tanto quanto latinos
 * SOLUÃ‡ÃƒO: Priorizar SMS como primÃ¡rio, WhatsApp como secundÃ¡rio
 */

interface CustomerCommunicationPreference {
  primary: 'sms' | 'whatsapp' | 'email' | 'app';
  secondary?: 'sms' | 'whatsapp' | 'email';
  phoneNumber: string;
  email: string;
}

// AUTO-DETECT baseado em country code
function detectPreferredChannel(phone: string): 'sms' | 'whatsapp' {
  const countryCode = phone.substring(0, 3);
  
  if (countryCode === '+1') {
    // USA/Canada = SMS preferred
    return 'sms';
  } else if (['+55', '+52', '+54', '+51'].includes(countryCode)) {
    // Brasil, Mexico, Argentina, Peru = WhatsApp
    return 'whatsapp';
  }
  
  return 'sms'; // Default
}

// CANAIS DE COMUNICAÃ‡ÃƒO (Priority Order for Americans)

const COMMUNICATION_CHANNELS_US = {
  
  // 1. SMS (Twilio) - PRIMÃRIO para americanos
  sms: {
    service: 'Twilio',
    pros: [
      'Todo americano usa',
      'NÃ£o precisa de app adicional',
      'Delivery instantÃ¢neo',
      '98% open rate'
    ],
    cost: '$0.0079 per message',
    implementation: 'Twilio SDK'
  },
  
  // 2. Email - SECUNDÃRIO
  email: {
    service: 'SendGrid ou AWS SES',
    pros: [
      'GrÃ¡tis atÃ© 10k/mÃªs',
      'DocumentaÃ§Ã£o permanente',
      'Pode incluir attachments (receipts, photos)'
    ],
    cost: 'Free tier disponÃ­vel',
    implementation: 'SendGrid/SES API'
  },
  
  // 3. Push Notifications (Se tiver app)
  push: {
    service: 'Firebase Cloud Messaging (FCM)',
    pros: [
      'Instant',
      'Rich media',
      'Free'
    ],
    implementation: 'Firebase SDK',
    requires: 'Mobile app installed'
  },
  
  // 4. In-App Messaging
  inApp: {
    service: 'Stream Chat ou Sendbird',
    pros: [
      'Real-time',
      'Rich features',
      'Professional'
    ],
    cost: 'Free tier available',
    implementation: 'Stream SDK'
  },
  
  // 5. Voice Call (Automated)
  voice: {
    service: 'Twilio Voice',
    pros: [
      'Para updates crÃ­ticos',
      'Idosos preferem'
    ],
    cost: '$0.013/min',
    useCase: 'Emergency notifications only'
  }
};

// IMPLEMENTATION EXAMPLE

async function notifyCustomer(
  delivery: Delivery, 
  status: DeliveryStatus,
  customer: Customer
) {
  
  const message = getStatusMessage(status);
  
  // Multi-channel simultÃ¢neo
  await Promise.all([
    
    // SMS (PrimÃ¡rio para US)
    sendSMS({
      to: customer.phone,
      body: message,
      from: process.env.TWILIO_PHONE
    }),
    
    // Email (Backup)
    sendEmail({
      to: customer.email,
      subject: `Delivery Update: ${status}`,
      body: message,
      attachments: status === 'delivered' ? [proofOfDeliveryPDF] : []
    }),
    
    // Push (Se app instalado)
    customer.hasMobileApp && sendPush({
      userId: customer.id,
      title: 'Delivery Update',
      body: message,
      data: { deliveryId: delivery.id }
    }),
    
    // WhatsApp (Apenas se customer preferir)
    customer.prefersWhatsApp && sendWhatsApp({
      to: customer.phone,
      body: message
    })
  ]);
}
```

**PRICING AUTO-CALCULATOR:**

```typescript
function calculatePrice(pickup: Address, delivery: Address): number {
  const distance = getDistance(pickup, delivery);
  
  // Base price
  let price = 35;
  
  // Distance surcharge
  if (distance > 10) price += (distance - 10) * 2;
  
  // Outside coverage area
  if (distance > 25) price += 20; // Extra fee
  
  // Time-based surcharge
  const hour = new Date().getHours();
  if (hour > 18 || hour < 8) price *= 1.3; // After hours +30%
  
  // Weekend
  const day = new Date().getDay();
  if (day === 0 || day === 6) price *= 1.5; // Weekend +50%
  
  return Math.round(price);
}
```

**PHOTO PROOF OF DELIVERY:**

```typescript
- Timestamp embedded
- Auto-upload to cloud (S3/Cloudinary)
```

### **3. COMPRAS DISCRETAS ($75/hora)**

```typescript
interface ShoppingRequest {
  storeLocation: string;
  itemsList: string[]; // O que comprar
  budget: number;
  paymentMethod: 'reimbursement' | 'upfront'; // Cliente paga antes ou depois
  deliveryAddress: string;
  specialInstructions?: string;
  estimatedTime: number; // Auto-calculado
}

// AUTO-CALCULATION
function estimateShoppingTime(items: string[], store: string): number {
  const baseTime = 30; // 30min base
  const perItem = items.length * 5; // 5min por item
  const travelTime = getTravelTime(currentLocation, store) * 2; // Ida + volta
  
  return baseTime + perItem + travelTime;
}

// PRICING
const hourlyRate = 75;
const estimatedHours = estimateShoppingTime(...) / 60;
const price = Math.ceil(estimatedHours) * hourlyRate;
```

```typescript
}
```

### **8. AGENDAMENTO / BOOKING SYSTEM**

```typescript
// CALENDAR INTEGRATION
Service: Google Calendar API

// Driver Calendar
- Synced com Google Calendar pessoal
- Blocos de tempo reservados automaticamente
- NÃ£o aceita booking se jÃ¡ ocupado

// Availability Check
function checkAvailability(requestedTime: DateTime): boolean {
  const deliveriesOnDay = getDeliveriesForDay(requestedTime);
  
  // Limite diÃ¡rio
  if (deliveriesOnDay.length >= 6) return false;
  
  // Conflito de horÃ¡rio
  const hasConflict = deliveriesOnDay.some(d => 
    isTimeConflict(d.pickupTime, requestedTime)
  );
  
  return !hasConflict;
}

// AUTO-ACCEPT / AUTO-REJECT
if (checkAvailability(booking.requestedTime)) {
  booking.status = 'accepted';
  addToCalendar(booking);
  sendConfirmation(customer);
} else {
  booking.status = 'pending';
  suggestAlternativeTimes(customer);
}
```

## ğŸ’° PRICING AUTOMÃTICO - LÃ“GICA COMPLETA

```typescript
function calculateDeliveryPrice(params: {
  type: 'basic' | 'confidential' | 'shopping',
  distance: number,
  datetime: DateTime,
  isRecurring: boolean
}): number {
  
  let basePrice = 0;
  
  // TYPE
  switch(params.type) {
    case 'basic': basePrice = 35; break;
    case 'confidential': basePrice = 55; break;
    case 'shopping': basePrice = 75; break; // Por hora
  }
  
  // DISTANCE
  if (params.distance > 10) {
    basePrice += (params.distance - 10) * 2; // $2 por milha extra
  }
  
  if (params.distance > 25) {
    basePrice += 25; // Fora da zona, surcharge adicional
  }
  
  // TIME
  const hour = params.datetime.hour;
  const day = params.datetime.day;
  
  // After hours (antes 9am ou depois 6pm)
  if (hour < 9 || hour >= 18) {
    basePrice *= 1.3; // +30%
  }
  
  // Weekend
  if (day === 0 || day === 6) {
    basePrice *= 1.5; // +50%
  }
  
  // RECURRING DISCOUNT
  if (params.isRecurring) {
    basePrice *= 0.9; // -10% discount
  }
  
  return Math.round(basePrice);
}
```

### **2. ALTERNATIVAS AO WHATSAPP (Para Americanos)**

```typescript
// ============================================
// COMUNICAÃ‡ÃƒO: AMERICANOS vs LATINOS
// ============================================

/**
 * PROBLEMA: Americanos nÃ£o usam WhatsApp tanto quanto latinos
 * SOLUÃ‡ÃƒO: Priorizar SMS como primÃ¡rio, WhatsApp como secundÃ¡rio
 */

interface CustomerCommunicationPreference {
  primary: 'sms' | 'whatsapp' | 'email' | 'app';
  secondary?: 'sms' | 'whatsapp' | 'email';
  phoneNumber: string;
  email: string;
}

// AUTO-DETECT baseado em country code
function detectPreferredChannel(phone: string): 'sms' | 'whatsapp' {
  const countryCode = phone.substring(0, 3);
  
  if (countryCode === '+1') {
    // USA/Canada = SMS preferred
    return 'sms';
  } else if (['+55', '+52', '+54', '+51'].includes(countryCode)) {
    // Brasil, Mexico, Argentina, Peru = WhatsApp
    return 'whatsapp';
  }
  
  return 'sms'; // Default
}

// CANAIS DE COMUNICAÃ‡ÃƒO (Priority Order for Americans)

const COMMUNICATION_CHANNELS_US = {
  
  // 1. SMS (Twilio) - PRIMÃRIO para americanos
  sms: {
    service: 'Twilio',
    pros: [
      'Todo americano usa',
      'NÃ£o precisa de app adicional',
      'Delivery instantÃ¢neo',
      '98% open rate'
    ],
    cost: '$0.0079 per message',
    implementation: 'Twilio SDK'
  },
  
  // 2. Email - SECUNDÃRIO
  email: {
    service: 'SendGrid ou AWS SES',
    pros: [
      'GrÃ¡tis atÃ© 10k/mÃªs',
      'DocumentaÃ§Ã£o permanente',
      'Pode incluir attachments (receipts, photos)'
    ],
    cost: 'Free tier disponÃ­vel',
    implementation: 'SendGrid/SES API'
  },
  
  // 3. Push Notifications (Se tiver app)
  push: {
    service: 'Firebase Cloud Messaging (FCM)',
    pros: [
      'Instant',
      'Rich media',
      'Free'
    ],
    implementation: 'Firebase SDK',
    requires: 'Mobile app installed'
  },
  
  // 4. In-App Messaging
  inApp: {
    service: 'Stream Chat ou Sendbird',
    pros: [
      'Real-time',
      'Rich features',
      'Professional'
    ],
    cost: 'Free tier available',
    implementation: 'Stream SDK'
  },
  
  // 5. Voice Call (Automated)
  voice: {
    service: 'Twilio Voice',
    pros: [
      'Para updates crÃ­ticos',
      'Idosos preferem'
    ],
    cost: '$0.013/min',
    useCase: 'Emergency notifications only'
  }
};

// IMPLEMENTATION EXAMPLE

async function notifyCustomer(
  delivery: Delivery, 
  status: DeliveryStatus,
  customer: Customer
) {
  
  const message = getStatusMessage(status);
  
  // Multi-channel simultÃ¢neo
  await Promise.all([
    
    // SMS (PrimÃ¡rio para US)
    sendSMS({
      to: customer.phone,
      body: message,
      from: process.env.TWILIO_PHONE
    }),
    
    // Email (Backup)
    sendEmail({
      to: customer.email,
      subject: `Delivery Update: ${status}`,
      body: message,
      attachments: status === 'delivered' ? [proofOfDeliveryPDF] : []
    }),
    
    // Push (Se app instalado)
    customer.hasMobileApp && sendPush({
      userId: customer.id,
      title: 'Delivery Update',
      body: message,
      data: { deliveryId: delivery.id }
    }),
    
    // WhatsApp (Apenas se customer preferir)
    customer.prefersWhatsApp && sendWhatsApp({
      to: customer.phone,
      body: message
    })
  ]);
}
```
